Securities

Critical Period, Cautious Long and Short Positions, New Public Bond Trading Gradually Decreasing 174

Fluctuations Resulting in a Drop of Thirty to Eighty Cents

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange and the public bond market appeared quite stable on the surface, but the trend was gradually downward. With no significant changes in the diplomatic situation, long and short positions gradually reached a stalemate. Except for the active forward trading, new trades became increasingly scarce. The fluctuating trend remained unchanged. In the morning's initial trading session, retail investors sold off, dropping slightly by thirty to fifty cents. In the second session, No. 5 bought several hundred thousand, rebounding slightly by thirty to forty cents. In the afternoon's initial trading session, Nos. 11 and 21 made slight purchases, rising another thirty to forty cents. At closing, sales of Nos. 34 and 40 surged, and market prices could not stabilize. Each bond gradually weakened slightly, some by twenty to thirty cents, others by seventy to eighty cents. As a result, prices fell again by thirty to eighty cents. Among them, spot salt tax and spot whole sixes, due to prolonged inactivity, fell by more than one or two yuan. These accumulated gains and losses have exceeded their time sensitivity and are insufficient to determine the day's trend. Currently, the Sino-Japanese problem has evolved from complexity to simplicity. Whether to fight or not depends on Japan's repentance. At this critical juncture of rising and falling, speculators inevitably hesitate, so market prices fluctuate uncertainly. The total transaction volume for the entire day was 6,762,000 yuan, including 1,000 yuan each for spot salt tax and spot whole sixes. Forward salt tax accounted for about 2.5 million yuan, demobilization bonds for over 1.1 million yuan, and various other bonds ranged from tens of thousands to hundreds of thousands.

American Cotton Usage

American Cotton Affected by Bank Suspensions of Cash Payments

Reports Still Indicate an Increase in New Cotton Fields 183

A New York telegram on the 17th reported on the cotton market situation for the week, stating, "The raw cotton market was loose this week, due to liquidation and sales by cooperative brokers, the Michigan bank's suspension of cash payments for eight days, and news of the closure of several small banks elsewhere. All of these events have created a disturbing force. In addition, the decrease in demand for cotton goods is also a reason for the loosening of the market. However, the decline in raw cotton prices has been resisted by industry buying around the six-cent per pound price for June futures. Market conditions have recently stabilized, and purchases are now waiting for the development of market conditions. The recent temperature in the cotton belt can be considered low enough to reduce dormant boll weevils. Reports from various locations still indicate an increase in cotton fields. The domestic agricultural relief bill has been passed by the Senate Agriculture Committee, but oversight is limited to those who grow wheat and cotton, and restrictions on farmland and production have been removed, making effective monitoring difficult. According to private sources in Washington, the Smith case has a better chance of passing, but some parties still doubt whether the case will pass."

Grains

Rice Prices in Hexia Up Ten Cents 184

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, arrivals were numbered twenty-five and twenty-six. Sales were piecemeal, with slight activity among urban and rural shop customers. Wholesalers remained cautious, with only traders going to warehouses to buy five to six hundred shih. Accumulated inventory in Pudong was light due to relatively scarce daily arrivals and better outbound flow, so selling parties were generally thinking of making a profit, and the market suddenly turned active. The price of Su Tong-style rice rose by about ten cents. Due to the limited supply of Qingjiao Baoxian rice, the market shape was still good despite weak wholesale demand. Nanhang-style thick and thin rice had balanced arrivals and sales and matched supply and demand, so market prices remained stable. Duyangjian was short of goods, and customers were holding onto them, so the rice was not affected by cheaper customer-pointed rice, and prices rose by about ten cents. The market for counterfeit silver yuan goods was sluggish due to scarce supply and slow sales, and there was no change. As for the five-dou and six-dou municipal measures used in the market, the outside world did not understand the truth and had misunderstandings. Therefore, after consultation among the northern and southern rice merchants, it was decided that only the five-dou municipal measure should be used, and the six-dou measure should be abolished to comply with the laws and regulations for unified measuring instruments.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, forty-one or forty-two boats arrived from Hexia. Sales of white keng rice were slightly improved in this street, with a lack of transactions in the surrounding countryside. Market shape weakened by another ten to twenty cents. Arrivals of thin rice were small and sales were balanced. Price shape was high and stable, with mid-quality rice slightly soft. Arrivals of early rice continued, and sales were relatively slow, with prices slightly lower. Yangbujian and Dujian had balanced arrivals and sales, with prices slightly soft. Customer-pointed rice was stable, counterfeit silver yuan maintained its momentum, and white yuan was weak.

Customer Xian Rice Sells Briskly and the Market is Stable

Rumors of Military Rice Purchases on This Street 185

Sales of customer xian rice were increasingly brisk yesterday. Both this street and Fuzhou trading houses had strong demand, with the total market opening close to 7,000 packages, the highest transaction volume in days. In the morning, Fuzhou trading houses bought 970 packages of Jiangxi late-season milled rice at a price of 8.60 to 8.50 yuan, and 767 packages of Hunan red rough rice at a price of 6.70 yuan. This street bought 476 packages of Hunan milled red rice at a price of 8.10 yuan, and 1,000 packages of Jiangxi late-season milled rice at a price of 8.73 to 8.55 yuan. Market conditions and prices gradually stabilized. At the afternoon opening, Fuzhou trading houses bought even more actively, continuing to purchase 533 packages of Hunan red rough rice at the same price of 6.70 yuan. This street had even stronger afternoon demand, purchasing over 2,000 packages of Jiangxi late-season rice at a price of 8.73 yuan, followed by 8.40 yuan, and over 900 packages of Hunan milled oil rice at a price of 8.40 to 8.50 yuan. It was said that the goods purchased by this street were procured on behalf of military needs by a certain firm in the South City, so the market situation at the close became even more stable.

Flour and Wheat Markets Show Tighter Conditions 186

(Tagged Flour) Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices for each month suddenly surged. Although there was no change in the quoted prices for foreign wheat, rumors of suspended Australian wheat shipments greatly agitated sentiment. In fact, although the situation in the north was tense, international transportation would definitely not be immediately affected. However, sentiment was easily affected, and because the current flour from each factory could be drawn directly according to the standard without additional charges, northern customers all started to draw and buy. The opening price for this month reached a high of 1 tael, 8 qian, 1 fen, and 5 li, which was 3 fen higher than the previous day. Prices for forward months also rose by one or two fen each. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, the tension remained at first, but then slightly subsided because Fufeng and smaller factories still had offers available, and the exchange rate had eased. There was a fear that foreign wheat shipments would continue to be booked, which slightly dampened sentiment. Fufeng and small factories had drawn and set standards for 170,000, and Fuxin had reached 150,000, so the price fluctuations of flour in the near term will depend on the drawing and loading situation in the later stages. As a result, this month's price rose by 2.5 fen compared to the previous day, March's price rose by 2 fen, April's price rose by 2 fen and 2 li and 5 hao, May's price rose by 7 li and 5 hao, and June and July's prices rose by 1.5 fen.

(Wheat Futures) Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat market in the morning and afternoon, the prices for each month showed an initial flat and then tighter trend. In the morning sessions, prices were flat because there was not much fluctuation in foreign wheat. However, the opening price for this month was as high as 2 fen, and forward months also rose slightly. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, the opening prices for each month were generally stable. Because most of the buyers were not in the industry, they were more inclined to wait and see at this stage, so even though the traders had a surplus of hedging, they were unwilling to offer more due to the situation, resulting in a stalemate. As a result, this month's price did not move compared to the previous day, March's price rose by 2 fen, April's price rose by 3 fen, and July's price rose by 2 fen.

There was no comparison for the remaining months.

Also, a telegram on the 17th stated that Chicago wheat was weak due to short covering and better export demand. The previous day's transaction volume was 10 million bushels. The market prices are listed on the left:

Closing Price Compared to Previous Day

May Futures 47.75 Up 0.125

July Futures 48.375 Up 0.125

September Futures 49.75 Up 0.25

Gradual Progress in the Soybean and Soybean Cake Market 187

Yesterday, the soybean market temporarily remained in a fluctuating pattern. Factories slightly resumed purchases, with a total of seven train cars of soybeans traded. Market shape showed a continued weakness in the Dalian market, so sentiment was uneasy. However, both arrivals and inventories were scarce, and soybean cake sales had begun, so the future of the soybean market gradually had hope of stabilizing. Soybean cake factories were still selling at reduced prices. Yesterday's transactions were goods returned by traders, so the market was slightly soft, but factory prices still needed to be in the range of 1 tael, 3 qian, and 6 fen. Guang trading houses bought 500 to 600 packages of red beans. Because goods were scarce, the market remained stable. The oil market showed a lively trend yesterday, and the market situation was also stable.

Sugar Market

Another Batch of Domestic Mianhu White Sugar Arrives 188

Yesterday, the sugar market's guild allocated a market price of 15.6 taels for No. 24 coarse sand white sugar, and only 100 bags were traded, probably because today was Sunday and there was no outgoing cargo from sellers. Both No. 20 medium sand white sugar and No. 890 Dutch red sugar were only quoted and not allocated, and the transaction was unusually light. Jianbing Da Laihua continued to open 35 boxes of Five Fortunes white crystal sugar at a price of 13 taels per cu, and the market momentum was firm. Although traders hoped to slightly reduce prices, the stock was thin, and they ultimately could not fulfill their wishes. Chao trading houses arrived with another 76 pieces of Mianhu white sugar, and it was said that the goods were better than before, and there might be a price increase. In addition, both Diaoqing and Chaoqing had no intention of making deliveries, and they did not continue to open.

North-South Goods

Black Fungus Opens Up Four Taels 189

Market Prices Rise Two to Three Taels

Black fungus has been scarce recently, and customer demand has been extremely tight. For example, Malanping fungus opened at 62.5 taels, and Sichuan fungus opened at 62 taels, up four taels before and after. However, on the sales side, Guangzhou trading houses were still in dispute due to the new scale relationship, and only Fujian Quanzhou and Xinghua trading houses had slight transactions, so market prices could not fully rise. Yesterday, the market price for miscellaneous fungus was 58 taels, and some were quoted at 60 taels, also up two to three taels from before, with a very tight trend.

Silk and Tea

The Artificial Silk Market Continues to Weaken 190

Only Over 300 Pieces of Chinese Silk Shipped to the United States

After the news of the drop in Japanese artificial silk prices was confirmed, the Shanghai European and American artificial silk markets were sluggish, and the exchange rate was tense, further weakening prices. Inland silk merchants were all watching the futures and spot silk markets. The market atmosphere was clear and weak. Yesterday, only Sichuan trading houses continued to buy 36 boxes of Grade B artificial silk for February and March at the guild. Prices continued to fall by five to seven qian and five hao.

Also, the sales of Chinese silk to the United States have not improved, and it is difficult to turn around exports. Yesterday, the American mail ship Jackson departed from Shanghai for the United States. Qianli and others only had 324 pieces of yellow, white, and gray silk loaded to New York and San Francisco.

Oil Market

The Momentum of Asphalt Price Increases is a Thing of the Past 191

In the past two weeks, the asphalt market has been quite strong. Hubei oil has risen by about five taels, and Zhejiang oil has risen by seven or eight yuan. However, because the goods that Hubei city pre-sold have not been delivered for a long time, and the source of goods has been extremely scarce, it has been necessary to temporarily stop spot trading and wait for the sold goods to be delivered before discussing transactions. The market has been quiet for a week. It is reported that what has arrived in recent days, in addition to delivering previously sold goods, still has no remaining inventory, so the price increase or decrease in the later stage is still unknown. However, because the momentum of Zhejiang oil price increases has been too strong, although it is not in danger, there are more sellers and fewer buyers who are watching, and the situation seems to be slightly weak. However, because the production area in the upper Yangtze River had a poor harvest year, and the amount of production has been greatly reduced, although there has been an arrival of goods in the market after the recent price increase, it is not as prosperous as in previous years. Also, the inventory of Hangzhou trading houses is thin, so even if the market is weak, the position is still solid, and sellers are really unwilling to sell at too low a price. Based on the current market, it is only a large price increase and a small loosening. Local traders and candle factories have no inventory, and very few goods arrive. Sales are not very smooth because candle makers are preparing for summer production early and are waiting and seeing. Also, since traders have no goods in hand, they are also unwilling to let the price increase too much. Currently, the asking price for heavy Jing is 23 taels, the asking price for flat Jing is 22 taels, 2 qian, and 4 fen, the asking price for high-quality Macheng goods is 22 taels, and the asking price for small Chao goods is 21 taels, 7 qian, and 8 fen. However, as far as previous years are concerned, soap factories are in the middle of needing goods, but it has not been heard that any has been purchased. If soap sales move, then the market should be discussed separately.

Hardware

Two Hundred Tons of Black Iron Sheet is Set 192

Yesterday, hardware transactions felt lively. Trading houses from Tianjin, Qingdao, Yantai, and various trading houses along the Yangtze River made purchases, so the transaction volume was still considerable. However, the goods purchased were mostly sporadic, so the market situation was even more complicated. Among them, black iron sheet had the largest volume, so the market goods had a lack of continuity. The standard skyrocketed, and the market price could be estimated at 9 taels and 5 qian per dan, while the thick variegated goods could also be opened at 8 taels and 7 qian and 5 hao per dan, but the market goods were extremely scarce. In order to prevent future shortages, traders all contracted forward goods with foreign firms. It was heard that 200 tons were contracted yesterday, and the price per ton was 10 pounds, 02 shillings, and 6 pence. It was determined that the contracted party was a certain British trading house. Yesterday, Tianjin and Qingdao trading houses bought over 1,000 boxes of tinplate, and the market price had very little fluctuation. Many people purchased British steel plate, but there were few market goods, resulting in few transactions. The market price was 2 li and 5 hao, and the market price per dan was 8 taels and 5 qian, 5 hao. The market price for half a fen was 6 taels and 7 qian and 5 hao, and the market price for 7 li and 5 hao per dan was 6 taels and 5 qian. The market price for one fen was 6 taels and 2 qian and 5 hao, which were all up from before. There were very few thick variegated goods offered, and the rest were around 6 taels per dan. Although the Yangtze River trading houses slightly purchased black iron nails and new galvanized wire, there were very few transactions, so the market price had very little change. In addition to inquiries, there was very little activity with new silver yuan angle iron, I-beam iron, galvanized iron tiles, etc., but due to good sentiment, there was no downward trend in prices. In addition, there were very few transactions in each market yesterday, and there was not much price increase or decrease.

Free Talk

Philosophy of Flying Birds 218

— Fan Zhongyun

Having been separated from Elder Fuyuan for several years, I recently had the chance to meet him on the streets of Shanghai. During the banquet, he was still drinking one sip at a time, and still joking in a calm and unhurried manner.

Recalling the gatherings of several years ago, it is truly nostalgic.

My deepest impression of Elder Fuyuan is his so-called philosophy of flying birds. But this is not the thought of an idealistic poet, but his view of women. He didn't originally have this name; I gave it to him. At that time, he was the chief editor of the "Contribution Ten-Day Magazine" in Shanghai.

Elder Fuyuan believes that women are like flying birds and should be allowed to fly freely among the branches and forests. If they are captured and confined in a cage, then although they may jump lightly and lively, and sing clearly and loudly, they inevitably lack vitality. Moreover, because they are imprisoned in a cage, they often make a mess of feces, staining clothes, becoming a great eyesore. Therefore, women are always more lively and charming on the street than at home, worthy of people's love. The reason why other people's wives are good is this, because we often meet them when they can fly relatively freely.

From the perspective of general feminists, this view is of course an insult to women. But in fact, it is not. This is precisely the harsh reality. Because until today, the existence of women in society is still just a bird; she is a plaything of men. The iron fetters of economics, in the form of marriage and family, bind her, making her unable to be free. Birds can still break through the cage and forage in the forest, but women can absolutely not open the nets of men. Career women are considered liberated, but they still inevitably use sex as a means of livelihood. School education should be able to break this bad habit, but in the end, it is still education for playthings or decorations, education for marriage and career. Why must company female clerks use appearance as a screening standard? Why must ministers and important people seek spouses from the universities they lead? And even why must female bachelors choose to marry gilded or silver young masters? Once we understand these things, we can reflect on ourselves more than halfway.

In short, true freedom must remove economic shackles. Otherwise, love is inevitably tainted with the smell of money, and marriage is simply a long-term profession of prostitution. Birds have two wings and the ability to fly. When birds become aware of these constraints, the realm of freedom may not be far away.

Remembering Elder Fuyuan, I wrote this the day after he left Shanghai as a memorial. And I wish him success in the educational cause of transforming society.

Speaking the Truth 219

— Zhang Menglin

People all know that Xiao Bonai is a comedian, saying that he is good at telling jokes. Xiao Bonai said, "I am telling the truth; the biggest joke in the world is telling the truth."

Speaking the truth 丨丨 this is Old Mr. Xiao's slogan that he has shouted loudly for fifty years. His essays, his novels, and his plays all center on this mission. For decades, he has tirelessly pointed out to us those heroes who tell lies to cover up their actions, the middle class who tell lies, the proletariat who tell lies, women who tell lies, governments who tell lies, etc. He exposes the comical nature of their inconsistency between words and deeds, calling on us to see that this is modern civilization.

The more selfish and self-interested people are, the more righteous and grand-sounding reasons they can come up with. The more corrupt and lawless officials are, the more they will talk about protecting human rights; the more pleasure-seeking modern men and women are, the more they will talk about dancing to save the country, and so on. So we often see many arguments in newspapers, advising these people to do what they say. Xiao Bonai said that these are idealists 丨丨 idealists who dare not face reality directly. People who are inconsistent in word and deed are because they dare not face the real reasons for their actions, so they think of a false, righteous, and grand-sounding reason to replace it. Similarly, those who advise them to do what they say are also concealing reality, ideally thinking that they can act as nobly as they say. Realists know that this is not the case at all. People are still in the process of evolution and cannot be perfect. These noble morals that they talk about are still out of reach. Therefore, human selfishness, greed, and pleasure-seeking are, of course, to be expected. But if we can face this reality directly, we can still come up with ways to improve. Humans are still constantly evolving forward. Therefore, Xiao Bonai's proposition is that people can act in any way they want, according to their instincts, but what they must not do is think one thing and do another 丨丨丨 speak the truth! What he asks of us is not to make our actions match our words, but to make our words match our actions. In this, Xiao Bonai has turned our inherited thoughts upside down again. He often plays this trick.

Then, according to Xiao Bonai's proposition, wouldn't good and evil be indistinguishable? Old Mr. Xiao answers this question from the idealist in "Major Barbara": "Good and evil! You think you can distinguish between good and evil after living so many years? Humph! What is good, what is evil? From Confucius to Socrates, for thousands of years, countless intelligent people have racked their brains, and they still can't come to a result. Do you think you can?"

So people can only do what their instincts dictate. Face the motives for why you do this. When you instinctively feel that this behavior is wrong, you will think of ways to change it. If you only use excuses to cover up this reality, you will never change in this lifetime, and you will not evolve into a higher animal in this lifetime. Then, there will be higher animals than you (what Old Mr. Xiao calls supermen) who will appear and treat you with the same methods you use to treat monkeys.

Xiao Bonai says that humans are indeed the highest animals now. However, biological evolution does not stop with humans, and therefore there is no reason why humans must be preserved. Why can't animals higher than you use the same methods to treat you as you treat other lower animals?

It is said that a year or two ago, an editor of a large magazine traveled thousands of miles to ask Old Mr. Xiao a question, believing that Xiao Bonai's answer to this question would definitely be of great interest to the world. His question was, in Xiao Bonai's opinion, who is the most precious person in modern times, the one who is most indispensable to culture and progress. He asked,

"If humanity suddenly suffered the fate of total destruction, and you, Old Sir, like Noah in Genesis, could use your power to leave a little of the human race, then who would you leave behind?"

Old Mr. Xiao answered with a mysterious smile:

"I wouldn't leave anyone behind."

Xiao Bonai is very pessimistic about modern humans but has great hope for biological evolution.

Now he has come to China, unfortunately at a time when imperialist Japan is invading us. This reminds us of his attitude during the European War. At that time, someone in England said of him, "The Allied Powers are fighting Germany on one hand and Xiao Bonai on the other." When the entire British people were denouncing the Germans, he unexpectedly denounced the British government. If this were in China, he would have been executed long ago.

His attitude at the time can be seen in the play "Heartbreak House." War is the result of modern civilization. Those affected by modern civilization are not just one country, but every country; not just one class, but every class. It is all of humanity that has been corrupted by modern civilization. Therefore, while the Germans should be scolded, the British should be scolded even more. When all the British people are scolding others, they forget themselves. Therefore, Old Mr. Xiao had no choice but to come out and tell the truth.

A second war is about to break out again. Perhaps Old Mr. Xiao will have to tell the truth once more! (The End)

The Black Girl's Quest for God (V) 220

— By George Bernard Shaw, translated by Yi Shi

"This is not an argument; it is a mockery," said the black girl. "You seem not to know what an argument is."

"Oh! I am the one whom the whole world acknowledges as having subdued Job; how can I not know what an argument is! I am simply laughing at you, child," said the old gentleman, who was very agitated but also too astonished to fully comprehend the present scene.

"I do not care if you laugh at me," said the black girl; "but you have not yet told me why you did not create a world that is all good instead of a mixture of good and evil. It does not count as an answer to ask me if I could have created it better myself. If I were God, there would be no tsetse flies [note]. My people would not fall ill with sudden diseases, grow terrible tumors, and commit all sorts of sins. Other kinds of snakes are able to live without a venom sac; why did you specifically put a venom sac in the mouth of a mamba?" Why did you make monkeys so ugly and birds so beautiful?"

(Note) A poisonous fly produced in South Africa

"Why should I not do this?" said the old gentleman. "Answer me that."

"Why should you do this? Unless you have a penchant for doing evil," said the black girl.

"Asking difficult questions does not count as arguing," he said. "This does not count as playing the game."

"A God who cannot answer my questions is useless to me," said the black girl. "Moreover, if everything is truly made by you, you should know why you made the whale as fat as it is in the pictures."

"What business is it of yours if I deliberately created him in an amusing shape for my own amusement?" he said. "Who are you to teach me how to make all sorts of things?"

"I am growing tired of you," said the black girl. "You are always in a bad temper. I do not believe you have ever created anything. Job must have been very stupid not to have recognized you. There are too many old men posing as gods in this forest."

She raised "Nob Kali" to strike him; but he nimbly slipped under the table. She felt certain that the table had already sunk into the ground because when she reached the table, there was nothing there. When she went to examine her sacred book again, the wind had seized thirty pages from it and scattered them like dust in the forest.

After this experience, the black girl was clearly troubled. She had not seen God: half of her sacred book was destroyed; she had twice become annoyed without receiving any satisfaction. She began to ask herself: had she placed too much emphasis on the white beard, old age, and pajamas as sacred symbols? It was fortunate that she met a very handsome white boy dressed in Greek clothing and with his head and face smoothly shaven. She had never seen anyone like him before. In particular, the outer corners of his eyebrows were raised and twisted, which she found both interesting and off-putting.

"Excuse me, sir," she said. "You have a pair of intelligent eyes. I am seeking God. Can you guide me?" "Do not trouble yourself so," said the boy. "Let the world be as it is; because there is nothing beyond the world. The end of all roads is the grave, which is the gate of nothingness; in the shadows of nothingness, everything is illusory. Take my advice, do not seek beyond the tip of your nose. You will always know what is beyond this; knowing this, you will be happy and hopeful."

Go Back and Tell Your Mother 221

— Yang Qiu

When Shaw was in Hong Kong, he said to a Reuters reporter: "Why is it that no one in the Chinese press has interviewed me? Are they so young as to not know me?" These two sentences are truly stinging and make us feel uncomfortable! But perhaps our Mr. Shaw has forgotten the lesson that a little girl in the Soviet Union gave him a few years ago. The story is like this:

When Shaw was in the Soviet Union a few years ago, one day, he played with a little girl named ××× for a long time. When they parted, Shaw said to her, "Go back and tell your mother that the one who played with you today was the world-famous George Bernard Shaw." But this little girl was after all too "young," and she didn't recognize who Shaw was. She immediately and without hesitation followed Shaw's tone and said to Shaw, "You also go back and tell your mother that the one who played with you today was ××× girl!"

Shaw hasn't forgotten this story, has he!

Talking About Shaw (Continued) 222

— Lin Yutang

(3) Shaw on Jesus

According to Shaw (preface to "Androcles and the Lion"), Jesus was a revolutionary idealist and the ancestor of communal ownership of wives. Shaw's view, according to Henry, is that the more the world progresses, the more it proves the greatness of Jesus's teachings. According to Shaw's interpretation, Jesus's teachings generally have four points, the second of which is:

"Abolish property and merge it into the public. Your work should be completely detached from remuneration. If you let a child go hungry, you are letting God go hungry. Set aside all concerns about tomorrow's clothing and food, because you cannot serve two masters: God and Mammon." The fourth is: "Abolish the ties of your family. All mothers in the world are like the mother who bore you. All people in the world are like brothers and sisters who share the same womb as you. Do not waste your time on funerals: pay attention to life, not death: fish in the sea are as good as fish on the beach, and even better. The kingdom of heaven is within you, and in the kingdom of heaven, there is no marriage, because you cannot serve two masters in your life: God and the person you marry or marry to."

However, Shaw absolutely rejects the legends that Jesus was Christ, claimed to be the Son of God, and could be resurrected and ascend to heaven. What is even more novel is that he does not believe that Jesus's personality was gentle. He can be said to be kind, loving, humane, tragic, and philosophical, but he cannot be said to be gentle. Shaw said:

"Calling Jesus gentle, humble, and meek is a despicable modern fabrication, which has no basis in the Gospels."

In fact, the great personalities of the East and the West have been misunderstood by petty people. Even our Confucius could ever be gentle, respectful, frugal, and yielding? He resembled Yang Hu, how could he be gentle? He was extravagant on one hand, and on the other hand, he wanted to go to see Gongshan Furao, who rebelled by extravagance; he also deceived the people of Pu into leaving Wei and breaking out of the siege, and after breaking out of the siege, he went to Wei and advocated attacking Pu, how could he be good? It was fine if he didn't see Ru Bei, but he had to pick up the zither and sing, making it difficult for people to be comfortable, how could he be respectful? He lived in thick fox and badger furs, and ate nothing, ate nothing, how could he be frugal? He refused to sell his carriage to bury Yan Hui, how could he be yielding? Therefore, we can only learn from Mencius and say: "However, without me, there would be no you." If we are willing to reread the Analects without wearing glasses, Confucius's personality will naturally come alive on the page.

Ministry of Education News 224

A summary of recent news from the Ministry of Education is as follows: (1) A telegram replied to the Hunan Education Department, stating that the Party doctrine courses in normal schools and vocational schools should not be changed for the time being. The compilation of Party doctrine in elementary schools should be incorporated into the curriculum standards of each subject and should be handled in accordance with this Ministry's Order No. 10388. (2) An instruction to the Sichuan Education Department approved the filing of Datong Middle School, but there were still points to be handled according to the order, which should be complied with. (3) An instruction to the Hubei Education Department stated that the submitted implementation plan for short-term compulsory education in Yingshan County failed to formulate specific measures and should be redrafted. (4) An instruction from the Executive Yuan stated that the request to urge the allocation of arrears for Chinese government-funded students at Columbia University had been ordered to the Ministry of Finance for verification and reply. (5) An instruction to the Xinjiang Education Department ordered the distribution of 4,000 copies of the first volume of the Chinese-Hui bilingual short-term elementary school textbook to the Hui schools in the province for application and ordered that the distribution situation be reported for future reference. (6) An instruction to the Jiangsu Education Department approved the filing of the submitted practical junior commercial school's regulations on internship methods and the establishment of stores, which were deemed satisfactory.

Ministry of Education Issues Chinese-Hui Bilingual Textbooks 225

The first volume of a type of Chinese-Hui bilingual short-term elementary school textbook translated and printed by the Ministry of Education has now been completed and bound. Yesterday, 4,000 copies were distributed with an instruction to the Xinjiang Provincial Education Department to distribute them to various Hui schools within its jurisdiction for application. Southwest Education Reform Committee Revises General Outline of Academic System for All Levels

Elementary and Middle Schools Set at Five Years Each, Universities Set at Three to Five Years, Four Semesters Per Academic Year, One Week Vacation at the End of Each Semester 226

丨The Committee Also Sent a Letter Requesting the Allocation of Boxer Indemnity Funds to Run Education in South China丨

(Guangzhou Correspondence) The Southwest Education Reform Committee previously resolved to reform the academic system and abolish winter and summer vacations, changing the length of schooling at all levels. After recent research, it was determined that the original reform plan still needed to be revised. Yesterday, the ninth meeting was held to revise and pass the draft general outline of the academic system and the implementing rules of the general outline of the academic system. The allocation of Boxer Indemnity funds was also discussed for running education in the Southwest. It was resolved that the committee would send a letter to the custodian of the Boxer Indemnity funds to request that a portion of the Boxer Indemnity funds be allocated for running education in South China. The revised general outline of the academic system and the implementing rules are recorded separately below.

General Outline 227

Article 1: This general outline is formulated based on the resolution of the eighth meeting of the Education Reform Committee. Article 2: The length of schooling for elementary schools is set at five years. The first three years are for junior elementary school, and the last two years are for senior elementary school. In areas where a full five-year elementary school cannot be established, a junior elementary school may be established separately. Compulsory education is set at three years. Article 3: The length of schooling for middle schools is set at five years. The first three years are for junior middle school, and the last two years are for senior middle school. Junior middle schools may be established separately. Senior middle schools should be established together with junior middle schools. The curriculum for the final year of junior middle school is divided into a general group and a vocational group. Students who do not intend to continue their studies after graduation should choose the vocational group. Article 4: The length of schooling for universities is set at three to five years. Article 5: Each academic year is divided into four semesters, each semester lasting approximately thirteen weeks. A one-week vacation may be taken at the end of each semester to handle the end of the upper semester and the start of the lower semester. Article 6: All current education laws and regulations that do not conflict with this general outline shall remain temporarily effective until they are revised. Article 7: The implementing rules of this academic system will be formulated separately.

Implementing Rules 228

Article 1: The scope and date of implementation of this academic system shall be determined by the chief administrative officer of education. Article 2: Within the 22nd year, one university, one middle school, and four elementary schools should be selected in the province, and four middle schools and eight elementary schools should be selected in the county and city to serve as experiments for the new academic system. Article 3: The beginning of the academic year for all levels of schools is July. Article 4: Graduation examinations for all levels of schools may be held one month in advance. Article 4: During the experimental period, the chief administrative officer of education should submit the experimental results for review. If they are found to be excellent, the scope of the new academic system's experiment should be expanded to all schools when schools begin at all levels within three years. Article 7: These detailed rules shall take effect from the date of promulgation. (Evening of February 13)

Ministry of Education Investigates Situation of Universities in Beiping 229

丨Only One-Tenth of Students Applied for Leave Before Vacation

Since the Yuguan Incident, the situation of students in various universities in Beiping escaping from exams to return home or leaving early for vacation, as well as the current state of the schools, has attracted much attention from all sides. The central government has also repeatedly sent letters to the Ministry of Education requesting it to investigate and reply so that it can review and handle the matter. On the 16th, the Ministry of Education again received a letter from the Central Public Guidance Committee requesting it to "strictly order the authorities of various universities in Beiping to severely punish students who are overdue in returning to school." After approving the letter, the Ministry of Education has telegraphed various universities in Beiping to promptly report the situation of the start of school and classes. It is heard that the Ministry of Education will deliberate on the situation of each school after receiving the replies and handle them separately. Now, based on what is known from the investigation, the process of this matter is described in detail below.

Reply Regarding the Transfer of Educational Expenses to Military Needs for Resistance Against Japan 230

The Central Government, based on the petition from Chen Du-xue and others, citizens of Beiping, requesting the suspension of educational funding for national schools in Beiping during class suspensions and the transfer of said funds to military needs for resistance against Japan, had sent a letter to the Ministry of Education for investigation and reply. (The Ministry of Education replied to the Central Secretariat on the 16th, stating, "Regarding this case, the Ministry previously, last month, based on reports in various newspapers about alarms at Yuguan, found that some universities in Beiping had students fleeing exams and leaving school, and classes being dismissed early. Investigations confirmed these events. University students are the backbone of the nation, and it is unacceptable for them to be alarmed and disrupt school regulations, and the school authorities did not report this, which is tantamount to condoning such behavior. Therefore, we have sent a telegram instructing the schools to report truthfully and in detail the circumstances of the students fleeing exams and early dismissal, so that we may investigate and handle the matter, and to also report the start date of the next semester. This is of utmost importance." Due to the foregoing, we are replying accordingly, hoping that you will examine and forward this to the Central Government.)

Only One-Tenth of Beiping Students Requested Leave 231

After the Ministry of Education issued the telegram last month, it received replies from various public and private universities and colleges in Beiping, generally stating that only one-tenth of the students had requested leave due to the Yuguan alarm. All schools followed academic regulations and dismissed classes on February 11th and held semester exams. Some schools that did not have time to hold semester exams will hold make-up exams after the start of the semester from the 1st to the 8th of this month, and classes have now formally resumed one after another. As for whether all students have returned since the start of the semester, no report has yet been submitted to the Ministry. As for the Ministry of Education's punishment for students who requested leave, left school, or arrived late for the start of school, nothing has been heard yet.

Four Regulations for Primary and Secondary School Teacher Training Schools

To Be Announced Within Next Week 232

The regulations for primary and secondary schools, compiled by the Ministry of Education, have already been reviewed and approved by the ministerial meeting. However, because they are related to various other school regulations, a comprehensive plan had to be considered. After the two regulations for normal schools and vocational schools are reviewed and finalized, the four school regulations will be announced simultaneously. It is rumored that the two regulations for normal schools and vocational schools can be reviewed and finalized at the ministerial meeting next Monday (the 20th), and the four regulations can be promulgated simultaneously within the next week.

Minutes of the Shanghai County Education Bureau's Office Meeting 234

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 277th office meeting yesterday afternoon. All staff members were present, with Director Shi presiding and Pan Sheng-san recording. Matters discussed: 1) Education Committee Member Niu forwarded the case of Pan Song-san, principal of the Guanhang Elementary School, requesting a promotion and salary increase. Resolution: Upon investigation, the person in question only obtained the qualification of a regular teacher in September of the 19th year of the Republic. Since the promotion period has not yet been reached, the request should be considered at a later date. 2) Education Committee Member Lin forwarded the case of the Beiqiao Elementary School requesting supplementary funds to cover deficits. Resolution: Since this concerns the budget, it is inappropriate to approve. The principal should find a way to collect payments to avoid a deficit in the final accounting. 3) Education Committee Member Lin Dun forwarded the case of the Dongqiao Elementary School requesting temporary funding. Resolution: An appropriation of ten yuan will be made. 4) Education Committee Member Niu forwarded the case of the Wujing Elementary School requesting the addition of an assistant teacher. Resolution: Since funds are unavailable, the request should be considered at a later date. 5) The Ganlu Elementary School requested the addition of a grade level and the purchase of additional desks. Resolution: The temporary funds allocated to the school for this year have already been fully disbursed, and no funds are available for the purchase of desks. As for the addition of a grade level, it is also difficult to approve for the time being due to lack of funding. 6) The Jingze Elementary School requested the addition of a grade level. Resolution: Same as case 4. 7) Education Committee Member Lin forwarded the case of the Shangbin Elementary School requesting the purchase of additional desks. Resolution: Since the school's temporary funds have already been allocated, the request should be considered at a later date. 8) Education Committee Member Niu forwarded the case of the Pingjing, Shuangxi, Guan, and San Elementary Schools requesting the purchase of additional desks. Resolution: The bureau will use the remaining amount in the temporary fund budget of the three schools (33 yuan) to purchase desks and distribute them publicly. 9) The County Education Association petitioned for a joint exam of private schools by the relevant authorities. Resolution: The bureau will add its comments and submit the case to the party headquarters for discussion. 10) Education Committee Member Lin forwarded the case of the Wu Hui, Deng, Si Cunzhen, and Gang Elementary Schools requesting temporary funding. Resolution: The remaining amount in each school's temporary budget will be allocated to them in full. 11) Regarding the date of the school principals' meeting for this semester. We can use our strengths to attack the enemy's weaknesses. When the opportunity comes, victory will be ours. With four games remaining, except for the Four Captives, there are also Jinan, the British Navy, and Lancashire, who are all no match. The Group A championship is safely in Donghua's hands. "Promote sports and promote the national spirit" was the declaration made by Mr. Sheng Xuanhuai, the founder of Donghua in previous years, when it was established. Now it has been realized. How can we not celebrate together?

Shanghai Basketball Association Group A First Final

Shanghai University Suffers Miserable Defeat Due to Chaotic Lineup 257

| Western YWCA Wins 39-36 |

Shanghai University's Mere Four Points in the First Half Proves Fatal

Third Final in the Coming Days

In last night's first Shanghai Basketball Association Group A final between Shanghai University and the Western YWCA, Shanghai University's lineup was chaotic in the first half, and their shots were inaccurate, making them at a loss. On the other hand, the Western YWCA was like a tiger pouncing on its prey, incomparably brave, making Shanghai University unable to attack or defend. The more than a thousand spectators could only sigh and be disappointed. The Western YWCA scored a total of 22 points, while Shanghai University only scored 4 points. This score was truly unexpected. In the second half, the situation became very tense. Shanghai University transformed from the flustered and timid state of the first half into a vigorous army. The audience regained their smiles and cheered enthusiastically. However, because they were too far behind in the first half, they suffered a miserable defeat to the Western YWCA by a difference of three points. The score was 36-39. The referees were Zhang Guoxun and Shu Hong, and there were over a thousand spectators, making it the first grand occasion of this season's basketball game.

The Curtain Rises on a Lifeless Scene 258

Slightly after eight o'clock, the Shanghai University team first entered the arena, followed by the foreign players of the West China YMCA team, also in athletic attire. After some initial warm-up throws, the referee signaled the start of the game. Shanghai University immediately found themselves under constant attack, struggling to defend. Smith of the YMCA team made two successful shots from under the basket, bringing the score to 4-2. It seemed they could compete equally, and the atmosphere was naturally tense. Unexpectedly, Shanghai University was trapped by the tight defense, unable to execute their plays. Wu Guolin repeatedly attempted long-range shots, all missing their mark, and the situation quickly became one-sided. The YMCA team found opportunities on both sides, playing with ease. White, Smith, and Zeiger constantly attacked the basket, scoring repeatedly. Meanwhile, Shanghai University seemed lifeless, surrounded and unable to defend against the onslaught. The score became a staggering 22 to 4. Finally, Sun Baoqing managed to score a basket, ending the first half with the score at 22-4. The situation was so dire that onlookers sighed in disappointment.

A Resurgence Begins, the Situation Changes 259

After this heavy blow, Shanghai University tried their best to rally. As the second half began, they fought hard, and the situation suddenly changed. The score gradually narrowed, and the spectators cheered wildly, making the atmosphere in the arena intensely exciting. Sun Baoqing made two free throws, showing great spirit. Smith immediately responded for the YMCA. Feng Nianhua also added a basket. At this time, the YMCA team remained brave, showing no weakness. Zeiger also added two points, believing that Shanghai University was still under pressure and unable to perform well. After a tense period, the score difference was only ten points. The supporters shouted themselves hoarse. The spirit of Shanghai University grew even stronger, and Sun Baoqing became especially courageous. In the last five minutes, Shanghai University's momentum surged. Wu Guolin repeatedly attempted long-range shots, all of which found their mark. Sun Baoqing assisted the attack, making great contributions. Feng Nianhua and Qian Jingyong also fulfilled their mission. The team advanced powerfully, playing with great enthusiasm, and their passion for the game was still high when the match suddenly ended. Checking the score, it was 39 to 36, with Shanghai University losing by a narrow margin of three points.

See You Next Week for the Final Showdown 260

In the first final match, Shanghai University was defeated. The reason for their defeat was undoubtedly their poor performance in the first half. If they had made just two more baskets, Shanghai University would have won. Scoring only four points was truly an unprecedented record in Shanghai University's history. Was it simply fate that they were destined to lose yesterday? It is difficult to understand the reasons. However, the first game is over. The second final match will take place next Tuesday. It is hoped that Shanghai University will do their best to avenge their loss. As for last night's game, White of the YMCA team was the most outstanding player, attentive in all aspects, brave and composed, running and stealing the ball quickly and steadily. Taylor's performance was average, and Zeiger Smith missed many opportunities. His shooting was not very accurate. Pyott was as brave as ever. The entire team had a solid formation, working together seamlessly, without any weaknesses. For Shanghai University, Sun Baoqing was the most outstanding, scoring a game-high fourteen points. Lu Zhongen was a spent force, only able to strategize, but appearing flustered during the game. Feng Nianhua and Qian Jingyong suffered disadvantages in size, lamenting that they had no room to maneuver. Wu Guolin still showed potential. The entire team should strive for calmness. Idle Talk

What I Saw on the Street 264

— Zhan Lu

丨The Poor Seamstress and the Modern Girl丨

No one wants to pursue and depict the poor seamstresses from Jiangbei. Their clothing and profession are too unaesthetic! The dark black headscarf represents the color from Jiangbei, covered with a blue cotton jacket, "green and loose, like wrapping green onions." Below, she wears single-slit pants tied at the ankles, sitting on a portable bamboo chair, her legs crossed and stretched out. On her feet, she stubbornly wears a pair of outdated pointed-toe women's shoes, bending her head to do her sewing work in the evening sunlight. Next to her sits a treasure-blue basket filled with scraps of cloth, needle and thread, scissors, and all the necessary sewing tools. The words she speaks are always about lengthening or shortening something. Of all the people passing by who glance at her, you would be hard-pressed to find even one who notices.

Her hair is permed in curls that cost dozens of silver dollars each time. On her body, she wears a sable coat worth thousands of gold dollars. Below it, a glimpse of a colorful and luxurious robe. The heels of her high-heeled leather shoes are as slender and precarious as the tall stacks of tofu in old restaurants. Slender eyebrows, snow-white face, crimson lips – everything displays the power of cosmetics. A gust of fragrant wind, like her advance guard, passes by the poor seamstress, making the seamstress seem like dust, while this modern girl seems like a celestial being. How aesthetic this is!

The next day, the aesthetic modern girl passes by the poor seamstress again. Because the road repairs were not yet finished, the heel of her right high-heeled leather shoe caught on a jagged stone and broke off, turning into a lopsided shoe with one low heel and one high heel. She was truly embarrassed! If she wanted to go back, she couldn't walk on this one-high, one-low road. If she wanted to buy shoes, the "Queen Shoe Store" was half a mile away. She leaned to one side, waiting for a car by the side of the road, fully displaying the awkward expression of someone trying to show off and suddenly encountering misfortune.

The poor seamstress, while sewing, slightly raised her stone foot and said, "My shoes are made by myself and never break at the heel. Even if they are occasionally damaged, I take them off right away and sew them up in a few stitches. Why wait for a car or look for a shoe store?"

When the poor seamstress said these words, her attitude was leisurely, and her reasoning was sufficient. But the modern girl with the lopsided leather shoes became even more embarrassed! Alas! Her aesthetic image was bankrupt!

Street Angels 265

— Especially

丨What I Saw at the Intersection of Wangping Street丨

On the road, a crowd of people surged, each different, dragging their various bodies forward with the interplay of legs and feet. Even though the wind was blowing and the ground was wet and slippery, this did not diminish their courage.

The sky was so gloomy that it showed the darkness of dusk. At this time, at the intersection of Fuzhou Road and Wangping Street, a group of people with unusual expressions crowded together, haphazardly arranged on both sides of the road, the sound of laughter resonating in the air. Their clothing was very thin. Some were shivering, hugging their shoulders, and some were stomping their feet. Looking at their facial expressions, it fully symbolized their inner anticipation.

"What? It's already five o'clock, and they still haven't come?" A tall, thin middle-aged man said anxiously after looking at the clock in the store.

"They'll probably be here soon!"

"·······················"

Confusion, noise, wringing hands, scratching heads – all expressing the nervous anticipation of the people waiting.

"Ah, look, they're here!" The magic of these words instantly struck a chord in everyone's hearts. So, they stopped shivering and jumping, pushing each other to stand at the corner of the road, looking westward.

A person with a cloth bag on their back rode over on a bicycle as if flying. Without saying a word, they were immediately surrounded.

"Hey! Thirty copies!"

"I want fifty copies!"

"······················"

The person with the bag was busy handing them out to the people crowding around.

"Do you want the evening newspaper?"

"Want to see it? Important news from Jiugemen!"

All kinds of different voices immediately floated away from the center in all directions.

Fiction

The Fire of Youth 266

— Gu Mingdao

When Kaijun looked at her face, adorned with powder and rouge, and her scarlet lips, he couldn't help but think of the rumors from outsiders. Although he was an open-minded person, after seeing her, he still felt that she exuded charm. The ancients said: "Beautiful as peach blossoms, dignified as frost." That is a good balance. Now, she has the glory of peach blossoms and plums but lacks the sternness of frost. Like the wine of roses, filled with sweetness, it's no wonder some people are drooling with desire! After she greeted Kaijun and his mother, she went to Kaijun and smiled slightly, saying, "I have something to discuss with you that I need your agreement for..." Before she could finish, Kaijun was stunned and couldn't help but put down his pen, asking, "Auntie Ju, what do you want to talk about?" She smiled again and said, "My life is pitiful, as Brother Kai already knows, so I don't need to go into detail. I think that continuing like this is not a long-term plan. I really want to go out and find some work to solve my livelihood. I don't want to live such a boring life without any support, which is very dangerous. But my education is really insufficient, so I can't even talk about finding work. Therefore, from today onwards, I want to dedicate myself to learning, so that one day I can have some knowledge and find a way to support myself, so that I don't have to endure this indefinite suffering. However, I have no one to help me, no money to go to school, and I'm not young anymore, so it's hard to get in. The best way is to study on my own. Tutoring requires the guidance of a good teacher to succeed. Brother Kai is the best teacher. I have already bought an English reader, and I want to ask you to teach me for one hour every day, whether it's morning or evening, just whenever you have time. You are sympathetic to me, so you should be able to allow me to do this. If I succeed in the future, I will be forever grateful. I wonder what Brother Kai thinks?" As she spoke, her eyes were fixed on Kaijun, and her attitude was very sincere.

After listening to her request, Kaijun thought, "So, this is what it's about." She spoke so sincerely that people couldn't help but help. Moreover, as a school teacher, I teach people every day, so how can I refuse her? And, from a rational point of view, this is also a good thing. Imparting knowledge to a lonely and pitiful woman, so that she can find a way to support herself in the future, is naturally a work of immense merit and a bounden duty in terms of humanitarianism. If I were to refuse, I wonder how upset she would be? While he was hesitating and hadn't answered immediately, Kaijun's mother, who was beside him, also expressed her approval. Kaijun didn't even have room to consider before he hastily agreed. From this day onwards, there was a special female student in Kaijun's study. The time was not fixed, because she had to take advantage of Kaijun's free time, but it was mostly in the evening. In addition to tutoring English, she also occasionally asked Kaijun to guide her in Chinese. (3)

Respect for Women 267

— Xianxian

丨Not Valuing Sons Over Daughters丨

Westerners respect women. Women wear cloaks, men serve them, women go out, men open doors and wait, women sit on trams, men stand up to offer their seats. In whatever matter, whatever men can do to help, they may not slack off. This is a kind of golden rule. If they dare to deliberately violate it, they are not worthy of the title of great citizens of civilized countries. As barbaric as our Chinese people are, after students who specialized in etiquette return home from overseas to promote it, and with the practice of talented men from foreign companies, the status of a first-class barbaric country has been raised to a third-class civilized country. Making an effort to promote and carry out [respect for women] is not only a small contribution; it is truly a uniquely great achievement.

But, wait a minute. Is this civilization just a mere imitation of Western customs? In my opinion, it is worth studying and considering further. So-called respect for women, at its maximum, is merely for women who are alive – not to insult, underestimate, but to respect them. This kind of respect for women is acquired. Furthermore, all etiquette for women is ultimately due to customs and ritual teachings. It inevitably feels awkward, somewhat forced and contrived. We Chinese, not boasting, not lying, have books as proof. In the Tang Dynasty, in the general thinking of the masses, there was already the concept of not valuing sons over daughters. This concept is for the piece of meat in the womb. It is completely innate. Furthermore, this concept is a complete internal expression. It is definitely not just idle talk. Foreigners open their mouths and shut their mouths, saying, “Respect women.” But if they give birth to a prince, they fire 101 cannons. If they give birth to a princess, they only fire 21 cannons. How can it be as completely authentic as our country's concept of not valuing sons over daughters?

European and American countries have novel inventions. When Chinese people say that China already knew how to use it thousands of years ago, foreigners often use it as a joke, laughing so hard they nearly fall over, saying that Chinese people all have megalomania. But I am now saying again that Chinese people practiced the matter of respecting women earlier than Westerners. I wonder if the foreign adults or quasi-foreigners will laugh at me again?

Children's Paradise

A Prince Seeks Love 268

— Yinping

Once upon a time, there was a very clever prince. Princes and princesses from faraway lands all came to visit him because of his reputation. One day, he saw a very beautiful princess and really wanted to marry her, but although he was very clever, he did not know what love was. He very bluntly asked the princess: "Are you willing to be my wife?"

"You don't even know how to say any words of love, how can you be called clever, how can I be willing to be your wife?"

"I know everything, except love," the prince said.

"Then you should go and learn!"

So the prince left her to go and learn about love.

× × × ×

First, he met Spring. Spring was holding a water pitcher and wearing a flower crown, like a young woman. The prince asked her: "What is love?"

"Love makes you drunk," Spring weakly stretched her tired limbs and replied.

The prince walked on and met Summer. He asked her the same question. Summer replied: "Love makes you suffer."

Going further, he saw Autumn. Autumn remained silent, not saying a single word. She only scattered leaves in the wind, as if implying: "Love makes you sorrowful."

The prince went to Winter's side and saw her wearing snow-white clothes. Her words spoke in seriousness: "Love is destruction."

× × × ×

We know that this clever prince would not say things exactly as he heard them. When he arrived at the princess's place, he said: "Now I have heard a lot about love, and they all say that love is life, is happiness. Now are you willing to marry me and be my wife?"

So the princess became his wife.

Hopscotch 269

— Zhang Yian

Hopscotch is a common game among children in Shanghai. Its earliest origins cannot be traced, but most children who have grown up in Shanghai generally know how to play this game. I think this game is closely related to smooth cement floors.

Now, let's introduce the rules of the hopscotch game.

The number of players is from two to four or five.

Choose a smooth piece of ground. Cement floors are the most suitable. Use white chalk to draw several squares on the ground, either in one row or two rows. Each row has several squares. The number of squares can be determined temporarily. Each square is about two feet in length and width. These squares symbolize "houses."

Each person prepares a small brick or other object of similar weight and about two or three inches in size, such as a stone, iron piece, or copper piece.

Game Rules: The first player throws the small brick into the first house. With one foot raised, they hop into the house on one foot, then use that foot to kick the brick out of the house. Then, they hop out. While in the house, the raised foot cannot touch the ground.

After hopping out of the house, they pick up the small brick and throw it into the second house. They then hop on one foot into the first house, and from the first house, they hop into the second house. Then, they kick the small brick out again.

Afterward, each house is hopped over in this way until all the houses have been hopped over without breaking the rules. If the throwing, hopping, and kicking are all correct, that is the first success. They can then arbitrarily take a house (square). In this house, they use white chalk to write their mark. Others cannot step inside it when hopping.

Then several people take turns hopping in order, until all the houses have been taken. This is the end of the game.

This is the most common way to play hopscotch. In addition, there are other creative ways, adding some fresh patterns. These will not be described one by one here. "Hopping" is originally an action that children aged seven or eight to eleven or twelve like the most. This is very closely related to their physiology and psychology. The effect can satisfy them psychologically, and it can help them develop and strengthen physically and be lively in their movements. "Hopscotch" is a kind of hopping with rules, organization, and interest. It is worth encouraging and promoting. I think small schools in Shanghai could definitely dedicate a piece of land for children to play this game in the future.

It should be noted that when hopping, the front part of the sole should be used, and it is best to wear rubber-soled shoes.
