Casual Chats

The Way Out for a Nation "Without Culture and Without Organization" 270

— Pu

In England today, there are two globally renowned scholars. One is the 77-year-old George Bernard Shaw, who caused a sensation and recently left Shanghai. The other is philosopher Bertrand Russell, who lectured in China twelve years ago. We know that both are world-famous for their insightful observations. After traveling in China, Russell published numerous writings praising ancient Chinese culture, compiled into a special volume that sold widely. Unfortunately, the old man Shaw's time in China was too short, and the places he passed through were mostly Westernized areas like Hong Kong and Shanghai (he didn't even see the northern and southern districts of Shanghai, let alone the rural villages). Therefore, some people think it's difficult to expect him to give us any profound criticism. However, there are two points that he had already heard about before his visit—now that he has personally been there, especially seeing the literati and scholars in Hong Kong and Shanghai, as well as the bustling merchants and coolies on the streets. The first point is that China currently "has no culture to speak of." According to the words of Shaw published by our newspaper reporter yesterday, there are these few criticisms of China: "According to the meaning of culture, as explained by science, it is everything human behavior that can increase human happiness, especially the control of nature. In China, except in the countryside where one can still find a little culture, there is no culture to speak of. Today, China is importing many so-called 'cultures' from Western Europe that have already lost their effectiveness and are harmful to the public, such as the parliamentary system, educational methods, etc. What is the benefit of these?" What we need to further explain about this criticism is that Shaw's so-called "China has no culture to speak of" should be interpreted as "China's old culture is gradually disappearing, and new culture has not yet risen." This interpretation avoids ambiguity. Because Shaw has not seen the true face of rural China, he has not tasted any of the flavor of Chinese culture. What he criticizes is merely an intellectual imagination. However, this imagined criticism does not conflict with the starting point of his friend Russell's praise, because Russell traveled extensively in the interior and had considerable observation and exploration of our country's rural customs and inland habits. The object he analyzed was based on Shaw's imagined "countryside." However, now, more than a decade later, the condition of our country can be said to worsen year by year, and the collapse of the rural economy is especially obvious, which is perhaps something Mr. Russell did not foresee.

The second point that Shaw knows is the lack of organization among the Chinese people. Therefore, his exhortation to the students in Hong Kong was to call on them to have organization and planning in their revolution. In his remarks in Shanghai a few days ago, he also focused on this meaning.

Looking at the opinions expressed by Shaw yesterday, on the surface, he doesn't seem to have any special suggestions for the problem of the way out for this nation without culture and organization, but in reality, he has already given us a very clear and concrete hint. He said that China is importing Western European cultures that have lost their effectiveness and are harmful to the public, which means that if China wants to seek a way out for the nation, it should re-develop and promote its own "culture that can be found in the countryside"! Based on the scientific definition of culture, we should strive to advance along the path of jointly increasing human happiness. He said that the revolutionary method of transforming the status quo requires organized and planned struggle to be effective.

Seeing the current situation of the country's demise, families ruined, and the people living in misery, if we are unwilling to be "people awaiting death" and still have the determination to save ourselves, then we should express sincere acceptance of the hints given to us by this old friend passing through, and unanimously advance along the two paths of "creating a new culture" and "organizing to save ourselves." At this critical moment of life and death, we have no time to hesitate and wait and see.

Business Life

The Life of Female Workers Entering Japanese Textile Mills 271

— Xiang

Last year, because of a flood in my hometown, I fled to Shanghai. At first, I did small business, but in less than half a year, all my capital was exhausted. I had no choice but to ask someone to find me work in a textile mill, but it took a long time to succeed. Later, I spent three dollars and finally found a job in the Dakang Textile Mill in Pudong. There were so many people registering that day! It was simply a sea of people, so crowded that no water could escape, which frightened my timid heart. After registering, everyone stood in line, tall and short, like a women's army. At this time, Japanese people came to choose, no small feet, pointed feet were also dangerous, ugly people were certainly not wanted, and people with pockmarks on their faces were even more unwanted. Everyone listened silently to the selection, like taking the imperial examinations in the past. Those who were not wanted were pushed out of the line with fists. Those who were pushed felt disappointed and suffered physical pain, which was really infuriating. Then, doctors came to examine the body, using instruments to listen to our chests, looking back and forth, touching hands and feet, busy without end. Anyone found with even a small illness was rejected. After that, fingerprints were taken, small photos were taken, and questions were asked. After all the procedures were completed, cards were issued the next day, allowing them to start work, and foremen were sent to guide the work. The wages of these novice female workers are very low, but the work is very hard. When I entered the factory, I really broke out in a sweat! Now that I am working in the factory, I see that the female workers in the factory, whether novices or experienced workers, are often beaten and kicked by the Japanese devils, which is really frightening!

Apprentice Life

The Master's Wife 272

— Shang

"Hey! Is there anyone outside? Send one person in." A loud and shrill voice shouted from the kitchen in the back.

In fact, I had already heard it, but I still pretended not to hear and continued to sweep my floor.

It's not that I'm lazy. To be honest, among us apprentice brothers, I'm considered one of the more diligent ones! Although I can't say how diligent I am.

I really didn't want to see the master's wife's hideous and terrifying, man-eating appearance. Since I entered the shop, it had been a full ten months, but I had never seen her speak to us in a kind or pleasant manner. Her order had come again. I thought to myself, I'll pretend to be deaf, and one of my apprentice brothers will go in! But the fact was beyond my expectations. They all took the same attitude as me, doing their own things, and no one responded.

"Is there anyone outside after all!" The master's wife's urging order came again.

"X! Did you hear that? Your master's wife is calling you!" The accountant, Mr. Mao, held a water pipe in one hand and a paper blower in the other, walking out of the accounting room while blowing. He didn't call this one or that one, but specifically called me.

I couldn't bear it any longer. On one side, I busily responded, "Oh! Coming," and on the other side, I quickly swept the dust into a corner and ran in as if flying.

"What! Didn't you hear me calling you? Lazy thief!"

"No! I responded! I was sweeping the floor in the hall! Master's wife!"

Fortunately, I answered quickly and shouted "Master's wife," otherwise, another scolding would have been unavoidable.

"Go to Wantong Soy Sauce Garden and buy two dollars of sesame oil and one dollar of soy sauce, quickly!" She said, handing me three dollars.

I already knew that there were no good errands when called inside. The goose-feather-like snow was falling outside, and I had to go to the soy sauce garden half a mile away to buy oil and soy sauce. But, as an apprentice, what could I do!

Dragging out two greasy and dark urns from the dark corner of the kitchen, I held one in each hand, braved the snow, and walked out of the back door. The urns were slippery, and I had to squeeze them hard. The skin on the back of my hand, which had cracked, seeped out drops of blood. The snow fell on it, and the warmth melted it into water. After a while, my hands were all red, as if they had been painted with a layer of red ink. I wore a pair of overshoes on my feet, and walking on the snow, the frostbite was both painful and itchy. But, as an apprentice, I had to keep walking forward!

Far, far away, I saw the two large characters "Wantong" on the wall. My heart was filled with endless comfort. Although there was no coal stove or brazier there, at least it could give me a short rest. Because of the joy in my heart, I couldn't help but speed up my pace.

Slippery... the ruthlessness of the snow, just when I was about to reach my destination, it still made me slip! My hands and feet were numb, but I could barely get up. Looking back at the ground, a piece of red was reflected in the snow. Fortunately, I was okay. After inspecting my whole body, a piece of skin had been scraped off the back of my right hand. Luckily, it was numb, and I didn't feel any pain for the time being. But, damn it! The urn in my right hand was broken.

Page 22

I stared blankly at the pieces of the urn in the snowdrift for a long time, not knowing what to do. I thought it would be better to buy one outside than to go back and get a scolding from the master's wife. Feeling in my cotton-padded jacket pocket, the eight cents monthly allowance that Mr. Mao gave me half a month ago, there were still six cents here. But if I had to pay for the broken urn, where would the money for haircuts, laundry, bathing, etc. for the next half month come from? Otherwise, could I endure her scolding all day long? After thinking for a long time, "It's better to be honorable than wealthy." After all, relying on my courage, I paid for the urn and came back with the oil and soy sauce.

As soon as I stepped into the back door, I quickly stuffed the two urns into that dark corner and ran to the front hall without looking back. Sure enough, the voice of "Little devil! You're only coming now after so long, you must have been wandering outside" came from inside again.

I was really reckless. I got hurt, lost money, and still had to suffer her complaints. I couldn't wait to turn around and argue with her, but thinking about the disgrace of an apprentice returning halfway, a wave of resentment and hot tears were suppressed in my stomach.

Employee Cultivation

"Don't Try to Get a Free Meal, Okay?" 273

— Duo Fei

Slowing down customers can seriously damage business, which is something no one can deny.

I feel that we should assume that all customers who come to patronize us have good intentions, and there is no reason to treat them lightly. Although many customers come in, look around, and watch the excitement without intending to buy anything; or they pick and choose and ultimately don't buy a single item; however, in the near future, they actually have the potential to become our real customers. If we slight them, then we will lose this customer forever. Customers have the right to pick and choose goods, no matter how picky. If they ask this and ask that, we have an obligation to provide as much information as possible. We must not be annoyed and show a displeased expression. Some less attractive customers insist on rounding down when paying after the goods are wrapped. We can only explain politely and ask them to forgive us. If they say something impolite because they refuse to reduce the price, we can only consider them extremely ignorant and not bother to argue with them. What is the victory for us shop assistants? It is to be able to complete the transaction. Even if it doesn't work out, our goods are still there, and we won't suffer any loss.

Our attitude towards any customer must be humble, sincere, and patient. Not only should shop assistant service be like this, but it is also an indispensable virtue for us to be people.

Northern shop assistants, when customers enter, regardless of whether they know them or not, will definitely smile and ask intimately, "You are well! It's been so long since we've seen each other!" When customers pay, they will also say politely, "You don't need to pay, just take this with you!" Although this is inevitably excessive and insincere, it is not worth emulating, but their attitude is so humble! Many shop assistants in Hankou glare at customers who fail to agree on a price, saying, "Coming to get a free meal, okay?" The meaning of "getting a free meal" is to ridicule you for never having tasted meat and not expecting to get a free meal here. This is not only "slighting" but simply giving the customer a major insult. Customers cannot tolerate it, so they often end up scolding each other and even fighting. You want to do business but end up scolding and fighting with customers, isn't that a joke? Shop assistants in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang regions don't seem to have this bad habit, and even if they slow down customers, they won't slow them down to this extent. However, their cold and indifferent faces are enough to make customers suffer.

But the customers they slow down are mostly people who are plainly dressed and have a bit of a rural air. For the grand gentlemen, ladies, young masters, and young ladies who are gorgeously dressed and behave lavishly, not only do they not dare to slow them down, but they often have to prepare to endure their anger.

I feel that all customers who patronize us, whether they are high-ranking officials or beggars, are the same customers in our eyes. We should not discriminate based on the size of the transaction or the social status of the customer, holding a snobbish mentality. We must always take a humble, sincere, and patient attitude and deal with any customer in the same way.

My conclusion is that we should not slight beggar customers, nor should we flatter and be particularly flattering to the grand gentlemen. We don't need to smear "Stancombe" on our heads and "Snow Cream" on our faces, and be particularly ingratiating to ladies with oily tongues and slippery faces. As long as they are customers, we should treat them equally. At the same time, we must not forget the essential virtues of humility, sincerity, and patience!

Commentary

Educational Pain and the Commodification of Professions 274

— Wen Huan

In the abnormally developed society of today, due to the unreasonableness of the social organization, the general cost of living is gradually increasing. The broad proletarian masses are all busy finding jobs, and they have no time to study. As soon as a child is born, he is regarded as a member of the family's producers. As long as there is a place to eat, he is pushed into the threshold of the store, so that he bears the considerable burden that he should bear in the whole family, so as to reduce the burden of his father and brothers. Everything else is a secondary issue. Even if there are children with intelligence and qualifications who have the materials to study, they are exploited because of environmental reasons; or even during the period of studying, they have to leave school life and go to society to find their own lives. Under such a social organization, I don't know how many geniuses have been buried and how many young people have been ruined.

The opposite fact is that there are more people than there are jobs. As soon as students leave school, they immediately become unemployed. When they were in school, they were full of ambition to transform society, but now they are softened and sacrificed by society. In this dark year, all departments are invariably accompanied by the form of business combination and trustification. A young man who has just emerged from the wilderness is undoubtedly surrounded by heavily fortified walls and cannot find his way in; unless you have great connections. Invariably deeply mired in the situation of hitting walls. Don't see the recruitment column and employment column in the newspaper recruiting personnel every day. To put it bluntly, it's just collecting a large number of registration fees and skimming everyone's oil. The quota for recruitment has already been taken by those with great connections who have arrived first. Under such circumstances, it doesn't matter whether you are a foreign product imported from abroad, or a purely domestic product, you can't find a way out. This is obviously the disintegration of education and profession, "what is learned is not what is used, and what is used is not what is learned," which is its greatest characteristic.

From these two aspects, on the one hand, the opportunity to study is sacrificed because of finding a job, and on the other hand, graduating from school leads to the contradictory fact of not being able to get a job. This is clearly the product of the current social system, because the essence of the current society is commodity substitution. The reflection in education is also full of commodified content, making education the private property of a few moneyed classes, and the majority of the proletarian masses are rejected outside the scope of education. At the same time, the result of commodification makes education and production the same, regardless of the needs of society, and blindly mass-produced. Therefore, in the industry, overproduction is formed, causing the panic of unemployment; in education, overabundance of talents and a sharp increase in literati, causing the difficulty of finding a job. Therefore, this is a fundamental social problem, which requires a thorough solution, so that this unreasonable society can quickly collapse and be replaced by a reasonable and equal social organization. In that society, naturally there will be no phenomenon of oversupply. At that time, education will be shared by everyone, and as soon as students leave school, they will have work that they are capable of doing, and there will be no danger of unemployment, like in the Soviet Union now. But in the current stage before reaching that society, everyone must make the greatest efforts, within the possible scope, to obtain lofty knowledge and obtain a considerable profession, so as to remedy the deficiency in the current process.

Amateur Sports

Poor Man's Equipment 275

— Hui Zun

In the crowded trams heading towards the Bund in the early morning, I have often stared at the faces of each of my fellow passengers. I have often found that the first faces are yellow with a touch of pallor, fully expressing "fatigue and not healthy." Most of them (and me too) are small clerks in the business world, and driven by life, they have no choice but to move their tired and unhealthy bodies back into the office!

Of course, under the current world economic panic, compatriots in semi-colonial countries will naturally have a few more symptoms of malnutrition due to the tribulations of life. However, the fact that our compatriots have never paid attention to physical education is also a reason.

Pay attention to physical education? This presents another difficulty. First, in this Shanghai where land is so precious, except for the gardens of a few capitalists that can be used as sports fields, the courtyards of most people's homes are not even twenty square feet. It is impossible to take a walk, let alone talk about sports? Second, sports equipment, does not every item require money to buy? Tennis rackets, footballs, basketballs, iron dumbbells, arm-exercising springs... so many strange things to exercise the body, are not all of them expensive? How can we, the small clerks with a monthly salary of twenty or thirty dollars, have the money to buy them? Therefore, as for "sports," we can only sigh in vain!

However, we cannot therefore not exercise our bodies. We need a body of iron, even more than the rich, so in desperation, we have no choice but to think of some "hard training" methods.

In the fresh air of the early morning, the roads are lovably empty, with few people. During this time, we can invite a few like-minded friends to have a longer distance race. Without spending a penny, our two legs will first gain the foundation of health (people with weaker bodies can change to walking).

The legs are exercised, but the two arms still lack exercise. Here, I have come up with another "poor man's equipment." This equipment is shown in the following diagram:

A B C D E F

Explanation: A wooden handle

B Hard lead wire

C Beef tendon (a little thinner than a horsewhip)

D Iron-core pulley

E Wooden handle (pulley device in the lower half)

F Weight Use a bag of foreign flour, filled with sand and mud,

Because sand and mud can be gradually increased)

It costs about one dollar to make this equipment.

After it is made, it can be hung on the ceiling. When you want to exercise, hold A in one hand and E in the other, and spread your arms open with force, then slowly close them. Practice dozens of times every day. In less than a month, your two arms must be hard and strong, but pay attention to two things: ㈠ Don't hold your breath, ㈡ Don't shrug your shoulders.

Hard training! Build up health!

Self-employment Introduction

The Death of the Female General 276

— Zhi

丨One of the "Epics" of North Era丨

Lin Liying is brave, majestic, and beautiful,

But her beauty belongs only to herself.

Lin Liying has the spirit of a great man, and no man is worthy of proposing to her.

× × × × ×

Three thousand beauties paled in comparison to her, and a brilliant pen cannot describe her heroism;

One billion two hundred million oppressed people are crying out in pain, and she wants to use her slender hands to turn the tide!

× × × × ×

Her cherry lips were not born for kissing, because she wants to awaken the soul of the weak nation,

Her jade arms do not know how many bullets they have touched, but she is unwilling to embrace a man even once!

× × × × ×

One beautiful youth after another bows down at her feet, and one after another becomes a pile of dust in her eyes.

Ten thousand gallons of tears cannot break her heart; a valley full of gold cannot buy her love.

× × × × ×

She would rather let the wind and frost wear away her rosy cheeks and let the long journey cover her beauty.

She said: "A good daughter does not become a prisoner of pleasure, quickly play, this tragic military song!"

× × × × ×

The young female general is full of vigor, and the entire world is burdened on her shoulders;

But she never calculates her age, only lets youth slowly pass under the iron cavalry.

× × × × ×

Look! See her standing on the mountain, riding and shooting; the silver command knife gleams in the sun.

A bullet drinks its fill of the enemy's blood, and a roar makes tigers and wolves tremble!

× × × × ×

The "charge bugle" sounds for miles, and Lin Liying faces the enemy alone.

The world changes color, and the sun and moon lose their light! Dark clouds slowly rise from the sky.

× × × × ×

A large banner flutters in the wind on the position; thousands of elite soldiers are all surging with blood;

One hundred thousand allied troops respond from afar behind her; countless cheering crowds are clustered in the deep valley!

× × × × ×

"Lin Liying! Lin Liying! Lin Liying!" The brothers shouted her name and advanced;

"Lin Liying! Lin Liying! Lin Liying!" The enemy troops trembled with fear when they heard it.

× × × × ×

To shoot a man, first shoot his horse, to capture a thief, first capture his king, rows of rifles are aimed at her;

Fierce firepower cannot suppress her courage, "Bang!" A ruthless bullet penetrated her chest.

× × × × ×

The brothers held her up with tears; the stretcher team stumbled to the scene; the head of the medical team only sighed that there was no medicine to heal; "Is there any divine power that can take back her life?"

× × × × ×

But the smile is still lingering on her cheeks, and the gray lips are still trembling; "Now, I want to hand over the responsibility to you; now, you can give me a kiss."

× × × × ×

The earth-shattering cries can no longer wake her up, a star falls from the sky and disappears; but the ship of the world is moving forward forever,
